'https://fal.run/fal-ai/nano-banana-pro/edit'\\n    : 'https://fal.run/fal-ai/nano-banana-pro'\\n\\n  const falInput = referenceImageUrl\\n    ? {\\n        prompt,\\n        image_urls: [referenceImageUrl],\\n        num_images: 1,\\n        aspect_ratio: aspectRatio,\\n        output_format: 'png',\\n        resolution: '2K'\\n      }\\n    : {\\n        prompt,\\n        num_images: 1,\\n        aspect_ratio: aspectRatio,\\n        output_format: 'png',\\n        resolution: '2K'\\n      }\\n\\n  try {\\n    const response = await fetch(falApiUrl, {\\n      method: 'POST',\\n      headers: {\\n        'Authorization': `Key ${falKey}`,\\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json'\\n      },\\n      body: JSON.stringify(falInput)\\n    })\\n\\n    if (!response.ok) {\\n      const errorText = await response.text()\\n      const sanitizedError = sanitizeApiError(errorText, 'image_generation', response.status)\\n      console.error('[Directors Generate] 이미지 생성 실패:', sanitizedError)\\n      // 잔액 부족 에러면 throw\\n      if (isBalanceExhaustedError(errorText, response.status)) {\\n        throw new Error(sanitizedError)\\n      }\\n      return { url: null, storageUrl: null }\\n    }\\n\\n    const result = await response.json()\\n    const externalUrl = result.images?.[0]?.url || null\\n\\n    if (!externalUrl) {\\n      return { url: null, storageUrl: null }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Supabase Storage에 업로드 (supabase와 generationId가 있는 경우)\\n    let storageUrl: string | null = null\\n    if (supabase && generationId) {\\n      const filePath = `${generationId}/frame_${frameIndex !== undefined ? 15 : duration === '10' ? 10 : 5\\n    // ✅ 해상도 검증 (720p 기본값)\\n    const validResolution = resolution === '1080p' ? '1080p' : '720p'\\n\\n    const response = await fetch('https://queue.fal.run/wan/v2.6/image-to-video', {\\n      method: 'POST',\\n      headers: {\\n        'Authorization': `Key ${falKey}`,\\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json'\\n      },\\n      body: JSON.stringify({\\n        prompt: motionPrompt,\\n        image_url: imageUrl,\\n        duration: validDuration,\\n        resolution: validResolution, // ✅ 해상도 파라미터 추가\\n        negative_prompt: 'blur, distort, low quality, watermark, text overlay'\\n        // ✅ Wan 2.6: 프롬프트 기반 대사 생성 - generateAudio 파라미터 제거\\n        // motionPrompt에 \\\"character says '대사'\\\" 형식으로 포함되면 자동 립싱크 생성\\n      })\\n    })\\n\\n    if (!response.ok) {\\n      const errorText = await response.text()\\n      const sanitizedError = sanitizeApiError(errorText, 'video_generation', response.status)\\n      console.error('[Directors Generate] 비디오 제출 실패:', sanitizedError)\\n      // 잔액 부족 에러면 throw\\n      if (isBalanceExhaustedError(errorText, response.status)) {\\n        throw new Error(sanitizedError)\\n      }\\n      return null\\n    }\\n\\n    const result = await response.json()\\n    console.log('[Directors Generate] Wan 2.6 비디오 큐 제출 완료:', result.request_id)\\n    return {\\n      requestId: result.request_id,\\n      statusUrl: result.status_url\\n    }\\n  } catch (error) {\\n    console.error('[Directors Generate] Wan 2.6 비디오 제출 오류:', error)\\n    return null\\n  }\\n}\\n\\nserve(async (req) => {\\n  const origin = req.headers.get('origin') || '';\\n  const headers = corsHeaders(origin);\\n\\n  // Handle CORS preflight\\n  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {\\n    return new Response('ok', { headers })\\n  }\\n\\n  const supabase = createClient(\\n    Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') ?? '',\\n    Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? ''\\n  )\\n\\n  try {\\n    const FAL_API_KEY = Deno.env.get('FAL_API_KEY')\\n    const FIREWORKS_API_KEY = Deno.env.get('FIREWORKS_API_KEY')\\n\\n    if (!FAL_API_KEY) {\\n      throw new Error('AI 서비스 설정이 누락되었습니다. 관리자에게 문의하세요. (코드: CONFIG_001)')\\n    }\\n\\n    // Parse request\\n    const {\\n      generationId,\\n      action, // 'analyze', 'generate_images', 'generate_videos', 'regenerate_frame'\\n      frameIndex, // regenerate_frame용\\n      videoDuration = '5',\\n      videoResolution = '720p', // ✅ 해상도 파라미터 추가 (기본값: 720p)\\n      generateAudio = true\\n    } = await req.json()\\n\\n    if (!generationId) {\\n      throw new Error('generationId가 필요합니다')\\n    }\\n\\n    // 현재 레코드 조회\\n    const { data: generation, error: fetchError } = await supabase\\n      .from('directors_generations')\\n      .select('*')\\n      .eq('id', generationId)\\n      .single()\\n\\n    if (fetchError || !generation) {\\n      throw new Error('생성 레코드를 찾을 수 없습니다')\\n    }\\n\\n    console.log(`[Directors Generate] 액션: ${action}, ID: ${generationId}`)\\n\\n    // Action: analyze - 대본 분석 및 프레임 구성\\n    if (action === 'analyze') {\\n      if (!FIREWORKS_API_KEY) {\\n        throw new Error('AI 서비스 설정이 누락되었습니다. 관리자에게 문의하세요. (코드: CONFIG_003)')\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          status: 'frames_generating',\\n          current_step: 'analyzing_script',\\n          progress: 10\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      const frames = await analyzeScript(\\n        generation.script,\\n        generation.num_frames,\\n        generation.style,\\n        FIREWORKS_API_KEY\\n      )\\n\\n      if (frames.length === 0) {\\n        throw new Error('대본 분석에 실패했습니다')\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          frames,\\n          current_step: 'script_analyzed',\\n          progress: 20\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      return new Response(\\n        JSON.stringify({\\n          success: true,\\n          action: 'analyze',\\n          frames\\n        }),\\n        {\\n          headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          status: 200\\n        }\\n      )\\n    }\\n\\n    // Action: generate_single_image - 단일 프레임 이미지 생성 (타임아웃 방지용)\\n    if (action === 'generate_single_image') {\\n      if (frameIndex === undefined) {\\n        throw new Error('frameIndex가 필요합니다')\\n      }\\n\\n      const frames = generation.frames || []\\n      if (frameIndex < 0 || frameIndex >= frames.length) {\\n        throw new Error('유효하지 않은 frameIndex입니다')\\n      }\\n\\n      const frame = frames[frameIndex]\\n      console.log(`[Directors Generate] 단일 이미지 생성: 프레임 ${frameIndex + 1}/${frames.length}`)\\n\\n      // 상태 업데이트\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          current_step: `generating_image_${frameIndex + 1}`,\\n          progress: Math.round(20 + (frameIndex / frames.length) * 60)\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      // Consistency chaining: frame[0] image as reference for all frames (prevents drift accumulation)\\n      const firstFrameUrl = frameIndex > 0 ? frames[0]?.image_url_external : null\\n      const chainingRef = firstFrameUrl || generation.reference_image_url\\n\\n      const imageResult = await generateImage(\\n        frame.image_prompt,\\n        generation.aspect_ratio,\\n        chainingRef,\\n        FAL_API_KEY,\\n        supabase,\\n        generationId,\\n        frameIndex\\n      )\\n\\n      const updatedFrames = [...frames]\\n      updatedFrames[frameIndex] = {\\n        ...frame,\\n        image_url: imageResult.storageUrl || imageResult.url,\\n        image_url_external: imageResult.url,\\n        image_status: imageResult.url ? 'completed' : 'failed'\\n      }\\n\\n      // 프레임 업데이트\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({ frames: updatedFrames })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      // 모든 프레임 완료 확인\\n      const allComplete = updatedFrames.every((f: { image_status?: string }) => f.image_status === 'completed')\\n      if (allComplete) {\\n        await supabase\\n          .from('directors_generations')\\n          .update({\\n            status: 'frames_complete',\\n            current_step: 'images_complete',\\n            progress: 80\\n          })\\n          .eq('id', generationId)\\n      }\\n\\n      return new Response(\\n        JSON.stringify({\\n          success: true,\\n          action: 'generate_single_image',\\n          frameIndex,\\n          frame: updatedFrames[frameIndex],\\n          allComplete\\n        }),\\n        {\\n          headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          status: 200\\n        }\\n      )\\n    }\\n\\n    // Action: generate_images - 프레임별 이미지 생성 (레거시 - 3프레임 이하 권장)\\n    if (action === 'generate_images') {\\n      const frames = generation.frames || []\\n      if (frames.length === 0) {\\n        throw new Error('분석된 프레임이 없습니다. 먼저 analyze를 실행하세요.')\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          status: 'frames_generating',\\n          current_step: 'generating_images'\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      const updatedFrames = [...frames]\\n      const totalFrames = frames.length\\n\\n      for (let i = 0; i < frames.length; i++) {\\n        const frame = frames[i]\\n        const progress = Math.round(20 + (i / totalFrames) * 60)\\n\\n        await supabase\\n          .from('directors_generations')\\n          .update({\\n            current_step: `generating_image_${i + 1}`,\\n            progress\\n          })\\n          .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n        console.log(`[Directors Generate] 이미지 생성 ${i + 1}/${totalFrames}`)\\n\\n          // Consistency chaining: frame[0] image as reference for all frames (prevents drift accumulation)\\n        const prevUrl = i > 0 ? (updatedFrames[0]?.image_url_external || frames[0]?.image_url_external) : null\\n        const chainingRef = prevUrl || generation.reference_image_url\\n\\n        const imageResult = await generateImage(\\n          frame.image_prompt,\\n          generation.aspect_ratio,\\n          chainingRef,\\n          FAL_API_KEY,\\n          supabase,\\n          generationId,\\n          i\\n        )\\n\\n        updatedFrames[i] = {\\n          ...frame,\\n          image_url: imageResult.storageUrl || imageResult.url,\\n          image_url_external: imageResult.url,\\n          image_status: imageResult.url ? 'completed' : 'failed'\\n        }\\n\\n        // 중간 저장\\n        await supabase\\n          .from('directors_generations')\\n          .update({ frames: updatedFrames })\\n          .eq('id', generationId)\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          frames: updatedFrames,\\n          status: 'frames_complete',\\n          current_step: 'images_complete',\\n          progress: 80\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      return new Response(\\n        JSON.stringify({\\n          success: true,\\n          action: 'generate_images',\\n          frames: updatedFrames\\n        }),\\n        {\\n          headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          status: 200\\n        }\\n      )\\n    }\\n\\n    // Action: generate_videos - 프레임별 비디오 생성 (Queue 제출)\\n    if (action === 'generate_videos') {\\n      const frames = generation.frames || []\\n      if (frames.length === 0) {\\n        throw new Error('프레임이 없습니다')\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          status: 'videos_generating',\\n          current_step: 'submitting_videos'\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      const videoResults: Array<{\\n        frame: number\\n        status: string\\n        request_id?: string\\n        video_url?: string\\n        dialogue?: string\\n      }> = []\\n\\n      for (let i = 0; i < frames.length; i++) {\\n        const frame = frames[i]\\n        if (!frame.image_url) {\\n          videoResults.push({\\n            frame: frame.frame || i + 1,\\n            status: 'skipped',\\n            dialogue: frame.dialogue\\n          })\\n          continue\\n        }\\n\\n        // 원본 대사 사용 (Wan 2.6 다국어 립싱크 지원)\\n        // ✅ Wan 2.6은 한국어/영어 등 모든 언어의 대사를 자동으로 립싱크 생성\\n        const dialogue = frame.dialogue || ''\\n\\n        // 비디오 프롬프트 생성 - Wan 2.6 i2v 프롬프트 기반 대사 포함\\n        // ✅ createVideoPrompt가 \\\"character says '대사'\\\" 형식으로 변환\\n        const motionPrompt = createVideoPrompt(frame, dialogue)\\n\\n        // Wan 2.6 비디오 생성 제출\\n        // ✅ Wan 2.6: 프롬프트에 대사 포함 시 자동 립싱크 생성 (generateAudio 파라미터 불필요)\\n        const result = await submitVideoGeneration(\\n          frame.image_url,\\n          motionPrompt,\\n          videoDuration,\\n          videoResolution, // ✅ 해상도 전달\\n          generateAudio && !!dialogue,\\n          FAL_API_KEY\\n        )\\n\\n        if (result) {\\n          videoResults.push({\\n            frame: frame.frame || i + 1,\\n            status: 'submitted',\\n            request_id: result.requestId,\\n            dialogue: frame.dialogue\\n          })\\n        } else {\\n          videoResults.push({\\n            frame: frame.frame || i + 1,\\n            status: 'failed',\\n            dialogue: frame.dialogue\\n          })\\n        }\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          video_results: videoResults,\\n          current_step: 'videos_submitted',\\n          progress: 85\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      return new Response(\\n        JSON.stringify({\\n          success: true,\\n          action: 'generate_videos',\\n          videoResults,\\n          message: '비디오 생성이 시작되었습니다. 상태를 폴링해주세요.'\\n        }),\\n        {\\n          headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          status: 202\\n        }\\n      )\\n    }\\n\\n    // Action: regenerate_frame - 특정 프레임 재생성\\n    if (action === 'regenerate_frame') {\\n      if (frameIndex === undefined) {\\n        throw new Error('frameIndex가 필요합니다')\\n      }\\n\\n      const frames = generation.frames || []\\n      if (frameIndex < 0 || frameIndex >= frames.length) {\\n        throw new Error('유효하지 않은 frameIndex입니다')\\n      }\\n\\n      const frame = frames[frameIndex]\\n      console.log(`[Directors Generate] 프레임 ${frameIndex + 1} 재생성`)\\n\\n      // Consistency chaining: frame[0] image as reference for all frames (prevents drift accumulation)\\n      const firstFrameUrl = frameIndex > 0 ? frames[0]?.image_url_external : null\\n      const chainingRef = firstFrameUrl || generation.reference_image_url\\n\\n      const imageResult = await generateImage(\\n        frame.image_prompt,\\n        generation.aspect_ratio,\\n        chainingRef,\\n        FAL_API_KEY,\\n        supabase,\\n        generationId,\\n        frameIndex\\n      )\\n\\n      const updatedFrames = [...frames]\\n      updatedFrames[frameIndex] = {\\n        ...frame,\\n        image_url: imageResult.storageUrl || imageResult.url,\\n        image_url_external: imageResult.url,\\n        image_status: imageResult.url ? 'completed' : 'failed'\\n      }\\n\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({ frames: updatedFrames })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      return new Response(\\n        JSON.stringify({\\n          success: true,\\n          action: 'regenerate_frame',\\n          frameIndex,\\n          frame: updatedFrames[frameIndex]\\n        }),\\n        {\\n          headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          status: 200\\n        }\\n      )\\n    }\\n\\n    // Action: merge_videos - 모든 프레임 영상을 하나로 병합\\n    if (action === 'merge_videos') {\\n      console.log('[Directors Generate] 영상 병합 시작')\\n\\n      const videoResults = generation.video_results || []\\n      const videoUrls = videoResults\\n        .filter((v: { video_url?: string }) => v.video_url)\\n        .map((v: { video_url: string }) => v.video_url)\\n\\n      if (videoUrls.length === 0) {\\n        throw new Error('병합할 영상이 없습니다. 먼저 영상을 생성해주세요.')\\n      }\\n\\n      // 단일 영상인 경우 병합 불필요\\n      if (videoUrls.length === 1) {\\n        console.log('[Directors Generate] 영상이 1개뿐이므로 병합 생략')\\n\\n        await supabase\\n          .from('directors_generations')\\n          .update({\\n            merged_video_url: videoUrls[0],\\n            status: 'completed'\\n          })\\n          .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n        return new Response(\\n          JSON.stringify({\\n            success: true,\\n            action: 'merge_videos',\\n            merged_url: videoUrls[0],\\n            skipped: true\\n          }),\\n          {\\n            headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n            status: 200\\n          }\\n        )\\n      }\\n\\n      console.log(`[Directors Generate] FAL.ai FFmpeg API로 ${videoUrls.length}개 영상 병합`)\\n\\n      // FAL.ai FFmpeg API로 비디오 병합\\n      const falMergeResponse = await fetch('https://fal.run/fal-ai/ffmpeg-api/merge-videos', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: {\\n          'Authorization': `Key ${FAL_API_KEY}`,\\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\\n        },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({\\n          video_urls: videoUrls,\\n          resolution: generation.aspect_ratio === '16:9' ? 'landscape_16_9' : 'portrait_16_9'\\n        })\\n      })\\n\\n      if (!falMergeResponse.ok) {\\n        const errorText = await falMergeResponse.text()\\n        console.error('[Directors Generate] FAL merge error:', errorText)\\n        throw new Error(`영상 병합 API 오류: ${falMergeResponse.status}`)\\n      }\\n\\n      const mergeResult = await falMergeResponse.json()\\n      const mergedUrl = mergeResult.video?.url\\n\\n      if (!mergedUrl) {\\n        throw new Error('병합된 영상 URL을 받지 못했습니다.')\\n      }\\n\\n      console.log(`[Directors Generate] 영상 병합 완료: ${mergedUrl.substring(0, 60)}...`)\\n\\n      // 병합된 영상을 Supabase Storage에 업로드\\n      const mergedFilePath = `${generationId}/merged_video_${Date.now()}.mp4`\\n      const mergedStorageUrl = await uploadToStorage(\\n        supabase,\\n        mergedUrl,\\n        'directors-generated',\\n        mergedFilePath,\\n        'video/mp4'\\n      )\\n\\n      const finalMergedUrl = mergedStorageUrl || mergedUrl\\n\\n      // DB 업데이트 (merged_video_url_external 컬럼 없음 - 제거)\\n      await supabase\\n        .from('directors_generations')\\n        .update({\\n          merged_video_url: finalMergedUrl,\\n          status: 'completed'\\n        })\\n        .eq('id', generationId)\\n\\n      return new Response(\\n        JSON.stringify({\\n          success: true,\\n          action: 'merge_videos',\\n          merged_url: finalMergedUrl,\\n          external_url: mergedUrl\\n        }),\\n        {\\n          headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          status: 200\\n        }\\n      )\\n    }\\n\\n    throw new Error(`알 수 없는 action: ${action}`)\\n\\n  } catch (error) {\\n    console.error('[Directors Generate] 오류:', error)\\n\\n    // Slack 에러 리포팅\\n    await reportError({\\n      type: 'EXTERNAL_API_FAILED',\\n      error,\\n      service: 'fal.ai',\\n      context: {\\n        functionName: 'directors-generate',\\n        endpoint: '/directors-generate',\\n      }\\n    }).catch(reportErr => {\\n      console.error('[Directors Generate] Failed to report error:', reportErr)\\n    })\\n\\n    return new Response(\\n      JSON.stringify({\\n        success: false,\\n        error: error.message || '알 수 없는 오류가 발생했습니다'\\n      }),\\n      {\\n        headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        status: 500\\n      }\\n    )\\n  }\\n})\\n\\n// 비디오 프롬프트 생성 헬퍼 - Wan 2.6 i2v 최적화\\n// ✅ Wan 2.6은 프롬프트 내 대사를 립싱크와 함께 자동 생성 (다국어 지원)\\nfunction createVideoPrompt(\\n  frame: { action?: string; shot_type?: string; emotion?: string },\\n  dialogue: string\\n): string {\\n  const promptParts: string[] = []\\n\\n  // 카메라 움직임\\n  const cameraMovements: Record<string, string> = {\\n    'Close-Up': 'slow zoom in',\\n    'Wide Shot': 'steady wide shot',\\n    'Medium Shot': 'gentle camera movement',\\n    'Establishing Shot': 'slow pan across the scene',\\n    'POV': 'first person view movement'\\n  }\\n  const camera = cameraMovements[frame.shot_type || ''] || 'smooth camera motion'\\n  promptParts.push(camera)\\n\\n  // 액션 변환\\n  if (frame.action) {\\n    const actionKeywords: Record<string, string> = {\\n      '걷': 'walking',\\n      '뛰': 'running',\\n      '앉': 'sitting',\\n      '서': 'standing',\\n      '웃': 'smiling',\\n      '울': 'crying',\\n      '말': 'speaking',\\n      '돌아': 'turning',\\n      '다가': 'approaching',\\n      '떠나': 'leaving'\\n    }\\n    const actions = Object.entries(actionKeywords)\\n      .filter(([kr]) => frame.action?.includes(kr))\\n      .map(([, en]) => en)\\n    if (actions.length > 0) {\\n      promptParts.push(actions.join(', '))\\n    }\\n  }\\n\\n  // 대사 - Wan 2.6 프롬프트 기반 대사 생성 (한국어 명시)\\n  // ✅ \\\"character speaks in Korean saying '대사'\\\" 형식으로 한국어 오디오 강제\\n  if (dialogue) {\\n    const cleanDialogue = dialogue.replace(/\\\"/g, '\\\\\\\\\\\"').trim()\\n    promptParts.push(`character
